# F1 Driver Peak ELO Ratings

This file contains the highest ELO ratings ever achieved by each Formula 1 driver across three categories:

- **Qualifying ELO**: Based solely on qualifying performance vs teammates
- **Race ELO**: Based solely on race finishing position vs teammates
- **Global ELO**: Combined rating (30% qualifying + 70% race performance)

## Peak Global ELO Rankings (30% Qualifying + 70% Race)

| Rank | Driver | Peak ELO | Constructor | Date | Season | Teammate | Teammate ELO | Race |
